 on July 25, 2016

Bracket
-------

 (8) oddseidank 







**(4) noloam, 2-0**






 (5) monkeyscantcry 







**(2) silviawataru, 2-1**

**(3) Hill\_Giant, 2-0**

**(1) HeyyQT, 2-1**

**(2) silviawataru, 2-0**

### Finals






**(1) HeyyQT, 2-0**






 (2) silviawataru
